And, a lot of people associate a diet that\xE2\x80\x99s filled with protein as a weight-loss friendly approach to eating. But why? </p><p>\xE2\x80\x9CWeight loss comes down to energy balance\xE2\x80\x94meaning you have to consistently <a href=\\"https://www.menshealth.com/nutrition/a28493677/what-is-cico-diet/\\">burn more calories than you eat</a>. <a href=\\"https://www.menshealth.com/nutrition/g23068259/high-protein-low-fat-foods/\\">High-protein foods</a> help out with<a href=\\"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC7539343/\\"> both sides</a> of the energy balance equation,\xE2\x80\x9D says <a href=\\"https://crossfit26.com/\\">Kim Yawitz</a>, a registered dietitian and gym owner in St. Louis, MO. </p><p>Ahead, all you need to know about protein in its regards to weight loss, and some of the best foods to get it from. </p><h3 class=\\"body-h3\\">Why Is Protein Intake Important for Weight Loss? </h3><p class=\\"body-text\\">\xE2\x80\x9CProtein has a few unique properties that make it especially helpful for weight loss,\xE2\x80\x9D says Yawtiz. Protein is <a href=\\"https://www.jomes.org/journal/view.html?doi=10.7570%2Fjomes20028\\">more filling</a> than carbohydrates and fat, making it easier to get and stay in a calorie deficit, which is required if you want to lose weight. \xE2\x80\x9CThere\xE2\x80\x99s also some evidence that the body <a href=\\"https://www.jomes.org/journal/view.html?doi=10.7570%2Fjomes20028\\">has to work harder </a>to digest and absorb protein\xE2\x80\x94meaning you could burn a few extra calories just by eating protein instead of fat and carbs,\xE2\x80\x9D says Yawitz.</p><p class=\\"body-text\\">Another reason that protein matters on the weight loss front is that this micronutrient helps protect against muscle loss in a calorie deficit, which is key on a weight loss diet, says Yawitz. \xE2\x80\x9CAesthetically speaking, muscle gives you that sculpted look, which is why many people go on a diet in the first place. But even if you don\xE2\x80\x99t care as much about your physique, you still want to maintain as much muscle as possible on a diet,\xE2\x80\x9D she says.</p><h3 class=\\"body-h3\\">Key Things to Know About Protein</h3><p class=\\"body-text\\">As Yawitz highlights, protein has less than half the calories than fat by weight, which means you can eat more while consuming fewer calories. That\xE2\x80\x99s a win if you\xE2\x80\x99re looking to slim down, friends. \xE2\x80\x9CSome studies have found that protein alone may not be enough to <a href=\\"https://www.frontiersin.org/articles/10.3389/fspor.2021.683327/full\\">prevent muscle loss</a> on a weight-loss diet,\xE2\x80\x9D she says. \xE2\x80\x9CYour best bet is to pair a high-protein diet with regular resistance training.\\"</p><p class=\\"body-text\\">If you need some inspiration on the resistance training arena, check out <a href=\\"https://www.menshealth.com/fitness/a19530279/resistance-training-to-build-muscle/\\">A Beginner's Guide to Resistance Training</a> and <a href=\\"https://www.menshealth.com/uk/building-muscle/a35780573/best-resistance-band-exercises/\\">20 Best Resistance Band Exercises for Every Muscle Group</a>. It\xE2\x80\x99s important to note that muscle loss accelerates when we get older. So older folks, in particular, should ensure they\xE2\x80\x99re getting enough protein. \xE2\x80\x9CMuscle burns more calories than fat (allowing you to lose weight while eating more food). Muscle loss can also <a href=\\"https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/31788969/\\">cause a lot of health problems</a> as you age, so it makes sense to preserve as much of it as possible while trying to lose weight,\xE2\x80\x9D says Yawtiz. </p><p>To preserve muscle mass, Yawitz typically recommends starting with 0.8 to 1 gram of <a href=\\"https://www.menshealth.com/nutrition/a39210389/how-much-protein-is-too-much/\\">protein per pound of body weight</a> per day on a weight loss diet. For instance, if you weigh 150 pounds, that amounts to 120 grams to 150 grams per day. \xE2\x80\x9CKeep in mind that eating too many calories overall will make you gain weight, even if those calories come from high-quality proteins,\xE2\x80\x9D says Yawitz. \xE2\x80\x9CYou may need to reduce your carb and fat intake, especially if you\xE2\x80\x99re eating a lot more protein than normal.\xE2\x80\x9D</p><p>Another thing that\xE2\x80\x99s important to keep in mind as you increase your protein intake is to drink more water. \xE2\x80\x9CIn<a href=\\"http://advance.uconn.edu/2002/020429/02042904.htm\\"> one small study</a>, athletes on high-protein diets were more likely to be dehydrated than those who ate less protein. In this study, the athletes didn\xE2\x80\x99t feel especially thirsty even when their urine showed markers of dehydration,\xE2\x80\x9D she says, noting that drinking water throughout the day can help you feel and function your best even if you don\xE2\x80\x99t feel parched, plus \xE2\x80\x9Cit<a href=\\"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC2929932/\\"> may even help</a> with your weight muscle mass, Yawitz typically recommends starting with 0.8-1 gram of <a href=\\"https://www.menshealth.com/nutrition/a39210389/how-much-protein-is-too-much/\\">protein per pound of body weight</a> per day on a weight loss diet. For instance, if you weigh 150 pounds, that amounts to 120 grams to 150 grams per day. \xE2\x80\x9CKeep in mind that eating too many calories overall will make you gain weight, even if those calories come from high-quality proteins,\xE2\x80\x9D says Yawitz. \xE2\x80\x9CYou may need to reduce your carb and fat intake, especially if you\xE2\x80\x99re eating a lot more protein than normal.\xE2\x80\x9D </p><p>Another thing that\xE2\x80\x99s important to keep in mind as you increase your protein intake is to drink more water. \xE2\x80\x9CIn<a href=\\"http://advance.uconn.edu/2002/020429/02042904.htm\\"> one small study</a>, athletes on high-protein diets were more likely to be dehydrated than those who ate less protein. In this study, the athletes didn\xE2\x80\x99t feel especially thirsty even when their urine showed markers of dehydration,\xE2\x80\x9D she says, noting that drinking water throughout the day can help you feel and function your best even if you don\xE2\x80\x99t feel parched, plus \xE2\x80\x9Cit<a href=\\"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC2929932/\\"> may even help</a> with your weight loss efforts.\xE2\x80\x9D </p><p>Ahead, 16 such high-protein foods that can help with weight Skipping breakfast","body":"<p>The first step toward weight loss at breakfast could actually be eating more! \\"One breakfast habit that can lead to quick weight gain is skipping breakfast or not eating a balanced breakfast that's high in fiber and moderate in protein and carbs,\\" says <strong>Steph Magill, MS, RD, CD, FAND</strong>. \\"Fiber and protein help give you that full feeling, so you're less likely to reach for snacks an hour after you eat.\\"</p><p>Magill points out that <a rel=\\"noopener noreferrer external nofollow\\" href=\\"https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC6215927/pdf/nzy074.pdf\\">research</a> has shown you're less likely to eat more snacks in the evening if you ate breakfast in the morning. Regularly skipping breakfast","caption":"<p>When it comes to finding breakfast habits that can help you reduce and <a rel=\\"noopener noreferrer external nofollow\\" href=\\"https://www.eatthis.com/foods-reduce-inflammation-aging/?utm_source=msn&utm_medium=feed&utm_campaign=msn-feed\\">manage inflammation</a>, a great place to start is making sure you're eating breakfast in general. Crazy mornings and busy schedules make it tempting to skip the meal and just take your coffee on the go, but research shows there may be a connection between inflammation and skipping breakfast on a consistent basis.</p><p>A study published in <em><a rel=\\"noopener noreferrer external nofollow\\" href=\\"https://www.cambridge.org/core/journals/public-health-nutrition/article/habitually-skipping-breakfast-is-associated-with-chronic-inflammation-a-crosssectional-study/F9A58BE929CBAC60646B46B6641B93CD\\">Public Health Nutrition</a></em> found that habitually <a rel=\\"noopener noreferrer external nofollow\\" href=\\"https://www.eatthis.com/side-effects-skipping-breakfast/?utm_source=msn&utm_medium=feed&utm_campaign=msn-feed\\">skipping breakfast</a> could lead to higher concentrations of CRP, which is a C-reactive protein and common marker of inflammation in the body. These findings were more significant in older adults than in younger populations.</p><p>Skipping breakfast had an effect on those with a poorer diet quality, but it did not seem to have a significant impact on those with better diet quality. For this reason, you should always look at the nutritional content located on the nutrition facts label,\\" advises Campbell.</p><p>When you do, be sure to \\"avoid any brands or flavors that are high in sodium, saturated, or trans fats,\\" adds Campbell. \\"You may also want to avoid chips with added dyes which can be used for coloring.\\"</p><p>With that in mind, you'll want to check out the following options, which are some of the unhealthiest chips you should absolutely steer clear of.</p><p>RELATED: <a rel=\\"noopener noreferrer external nofollow\\" href=\\"https://www.eatthis.com/unhealthiest-foods-on-the-planet/?utm_source=msn&utm_medium=feed&utm_campaign=msn-feed\\">72 Unhealthiest Foods on the Planet</a></p>","image":{"width":1200,"height":879,"quality":98,"url":"https://img-s-msn-com.akamaized.net/tenant/amp/entityid/AAUCotS.img","attribution":"\xC2\xA9 Provided by Eat This, Not That!","title":"4.
